CREATE TABLE tdf(
   id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY
  ,Stage          VARCHAR(3) NOT NULL 
  ,Date           DATE  NOT NULL
  ,Distance       NUMERIC(6,3) NOT NULL
  ,Origin         VARCHAR(31) NOT NULL
  ,Destination    VARCHAR(31) NOT NULL
  ,Type           VARCHAR(29) NOT NULL
  ,Winner         VARCHAR(41) NOT NULL
  ,Winner_Country VARCHAR(15)
);
